					var pogId = el;
					var guid = getGuidId();
					(rtbhEvents = window.rtbhEvents || []).push({ eventType: 'basketadd', offerId: pogId }, { eventType: 'uid', id: guid });

			var getGuidId = function(){
				try {
					var xg = Snapdeal.Cookie.get('xg');
					var xgVal = xg && JSON.parse(xg);
					var xgString = xgVal && atob(xgVal);
					var xgParts = xgString ? xgString.split('||') : [];
					var guidObject = (xgParts[0] && JSON.parse(xgParts[0])) || {};
					var uid = guidObject && guidObject.uid || {};
					var guid = uid && uid.guid || '';
					return guid;
				} catch (error) {
				}
			}
		</script>

	        <script>
function httpRequest(url, method, callback, isSync, data, timeout){
    var xmlHttp = new XMLHttpRequest();
    try {
        xmlHttp = new XMLHttpRequest;
    } catch (e) {
        var msxml = ['MSXML2.XMLHTTP.3.0', 'MSXML2.XMLHTTP', 'Microsoft.XMLHTTP'];
        for (var i = 0, len = msxml.length; i < len; ++i) {
            try {
                xmlHttp = new ActiveXObject(msxml[i]);
                break;
            } catch (e) {}
        }
    }
    
    if(!!timeout && !isSync){
        if (typeof xmlHttp.timeout === "number") {
            xmlHttp.timeout = timeout;
        } else {
            setTimeout(function () {
                if (xmlHttp.abort) {
                    xmlHttp.abort();
                }
            }, timeout);
        }
        xmlHttp.ontimeout = function(){
            if (xmlHttp.abort) {
                xmlHttp.abort();
            }
        }
    }
    
    xmlHttp.open(method, url, isSync ? false : true);
    
    xmlHttp.setRequestHeader("Content-type", "application/json");
    
    if(!!data){
        xmlHttp.send(data || null);        
    }
    
    xmlHttp.onreadystatechange = function() { 
        if (xmlHttp.readyState == 4 && xmlHttp.status == 200)
            callback(xmlHttp.responseText);
    }
}
</script>


<div id="ceeExp" class="hidden"></div>
    <script type="text/javascript">
        var getCookie = function(cookie){
            var cookie_start = document.cookie.indexOf(" "+cookie+"=");
            if(cookie_start == -1){
                if(document.cookie.indexOf(cookie+"=") == 0){
                    cookie_start = 0;
                }
            }
            var cookie_end  = document.cookie.indexOf(';', cookie_start);
            cookie_start = cookie_start > 0 ? ++cookie_start : cookie_start;
            var cookie = cookie_start > -1 ? document.cookie.substring(cookie_start+cookie.length+1, cookie_end) : "";
            return cookie;
        }
        
        var pin = getCookie('spin');
    
        var expData = {
            event : document.body.getAttribute('data-ceePageName') || '',
            appBrowserVersion : navigator.userAgent,
            appPlatform : navigator.platform,
            appType : 'WEB',
            pincode : pin ? pin.split('-')[0] : '',
            cookie  : getCookie('u'),
            catUrl  : document.getElementById('categoryUrlSearch')? document.getElementById('categoryUrlSearch').value  : undefined,
            pogId   : '',
            requestMap : {
                referrerURL : location.host + location.pathname,
                queryParams : location.search,
                keyword : document.getElementById('keyword')    ? document.getElementById('keyword').value      : undefined
            }
        };
        
        var callback = function(data){
            try{
                if(data){
                    var response = JSON.parse(data);
                    if(response.successful == true){                    
                        var actionsCount = response.actions ? response.actions.length : 0;
                        var scriptData = "";
                        for(var i=0; i<actionsCount; i++){
                            if('JS_action' == response.actions[i].templateStyle && 'JS_inline' == response.actions[i].templateSubStyle){
                                scriptData += response.actions[i].data;
                            }
                        }
                        document.getElementById('ceeExp').innerHTML = scriptData;
                        var scripts = document.getElementById('ceeExp').getElementsByTagName('script');
                        var scLen = scripts.length;
                        for(var j=0; j<scLen; j++){
                            eval(scripts[j].innerHTML);
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            catch(err){}
        };
        
        if(!!expData.event){
            httpRequest('/acors/web/getpageexperiments', 'POST', callback, false, JSON.stringify(expData));
        }
    </script>

                    <div id="filterAdTechComp" class="comp-filter-adtech hidden">
                            <script type="text/javascript">
    (function () {
        getCookie = function (a_name) {
            if (document.cookie.length > 0) {
                begin = document.cookie.indexOf(" " + a_name + "=");
                if (begin != -1) {
                    begin += a_name.length + 2;
                    end = document.cookie.indexOf(";", begin);
                    if (end == -1)
                        end = document.cookie.length;
                    return unescape(document.cookie.substring(begin, end));
                } else {
                    begin = document.cookie.indexOf(a_name + "=");
                    if (begin != -1) {
                        begin += a_name.length + 1;
                        end = document.cookie.indexOf(";", begin);
                        if (end == -1)
                            end = document.cookie.length;
                        return unescape(document.cookie.substring(begin, end));
                    }
                }
            }
            return null;
        };

        function bannerSwitchCheck(catPage) {
            var topBannerFlag = true;
            console.log(catPage);
            if (catPage) {
                topBannerFlag = "false" === "true";
            } else {
                topBannerFlag = "false" === "true";
            }
            return topBannerFlag;
        }

        getAdtechContent();

        function getAdtechContent() {
            var catPage = Boolean("");

            if (!bannerSwitchCheck(catPage)) {
                return;
            }

            var adURL = "https://sgb.snapdeal.biz/pub/getContent";
            var resCont = document.getElementById("filterAdTechComp");

            sendAjaxToAdTech(adURL, resCont);

            function getAdParams() {
                var pubId = "1";
                var rs = "html";
                var adSpaceId = getAdSpaceId();
                var siteId = "101";
                var pagetype = getPageType();
                var response_type = "banner_ad";
                var sdId = getCookie('u');
                var creativeData = "";              //todo
                var templateId = "bannerWeb3";
                var spin = getCookie('spin');
                var zone = getCookie('zone');
                var phn="";
                try{
                    phn=JSON.parse(Snapdeal.localStorage.getItem('authData')).mobile;
                }catch(err) {
                }
          		var pincode = (spin != null) ? spin.split('-')[0] : '';
          		var qparam = "";
                var email;
                var adParams;

                if (!!(email = getCookie('eid'))) {
                    email = email.substring(1, email.length - 1);
                } else {
                    email = '';
                }
                adParams = "?pubId=" + pubId + "&rs=" + rs + "&slotId=" + adSpaceId + "&siteId=" + siteId + "&response_type=" + response_type + getKeyCatValParamStr() + "&templateId=" + templateId + "&pagetype=" + pagetype + "&sdId=147342473456225597" + "&usedCreatives=" + creativeData + "&eId=" +  email+"&pincode=" + pincode+"&q=" + qparam+ "&zone=" + zone+ "&phn=" + phn;

                return adParams;
            }

            function getAdSpaceId() {
                if (catPage) {
                    return "sd-bn-340X288-1-1-1";
                }
                return "sd-bn-340X288-2-1-1";
            }

            function getPageType() {
                if (catPage) {
                    return "clp";
                }
                return "slp";
            }

            function getKeyCatValParamStr() {
                if (catPage) {
                    return "&category=" + getCategoryVal();
                }
                return "&keyword=" + getKeyWordVal();
            }

            function getCategoryVal() {
                var catUrlComp;

                catUrlComp = document.getElementById("categoryUrlSearch");
                if (catUrlComp) {
                    return catUrlComp.value;
                }
                return "";
            }

            function getKeyWordVal() {
                var keywordComp;

                keywordComp = document.getElementById("keyword");
                if (keywordComp) {
                    return keywordComp.value;
                }
                return "";
            }

            function sendAjaxToAdTech(adURL, resCont) {
                var xhttp = null;
                try {
                    xhttp = new XMLHttpRequest;
                } catch (e) {
                    var msxml = ['MSXML2.XMLHTTP.3.0', 'MSXML2.XMLHTTP',
                        'Microsoft.XMLHTTP'];
                    for (var i = 0, len = msxml.length; i < len; ++i) {
                        try {
                            xhttp = new ActiveXObject(msxml[i]);
                            break;
                        } catch (e) {
                        }
                    }
                }

                xhttp.onreadystatechange = function () {
                    if (xhttp.readyState == 4 && xhttp.status == 200) {
                        if (resCont) {
                            resCont.innerHTML += xhttp.responseText;
                            resCont.classList.remove("hidden");
                        }
                    }
                };
                try {
                    xhttp.open("GET", adURL + getAdParams(), true);
                    xhttp.setRequestHeader("Content-type", "application/x-www-form-urlencoded");
                    xhttp.send();
                } catch (e) {
                    return;
                }
            }
        }
    })();
</script>
</div>
                    </div>
            </div>

                        <script type="text/javascript">
    (function () {
        getCookie = function (a_name) {
            if (document.cookie.length > 0) {
                begin = document.cookie.indexOf(" " + a_name + "=");
                if (begin != -1) {
                    begin += a_name.length + 2;
                    end = document.cookie.indexOf(";", begin);
                    if (end == -1)
                        end = document.cookie.length;
                    return unescape(document.cookie.substring(begin, end));
                } else {
                    begin = document.cookie.indexOf(a_name + "=");
                    if (begin != -1) {
                        begin += a_name.length + 1;
                        end = document.cookie.indexOf(";", begin);
                        if (end == -1)
                            end = document.cookie.length;
                        return unescape(document.cookie.substring(begin, end));
                    }
                }
            }
            return null;
        };

        getAdtechContent();

        function bannerSwitchCheck(catPage) {
            var topBannerFlag = true;

            if (catPage) {
                topBannerFlag = "true" === "true";
            } else {
                topBannerFlag = "false" === "true";
            }

            return topBannerFlag;
        }

        function getAdtechContent() {

            if (!bannerSwitchCheck(catPage)) {
                return;
            }

                return adParams;
            }

            function getAdSpaceId() {

                }
                return "sd-bn-1240X110-2-1-1";
            }

            function getPageType() {
                if (catPage) {
                    return "clp";
                }
                return "slp";
            }

            function getKeyCatValParamStr() {
                if (catPage) {
                    return "&category=" + getCategoryVal();
                }
                return "&keyword=" + getKeyWordVal();
            }

            function getCategoryVal() {
                var catUrlComp;

                catUrlComp = document.getElementById("categoryUrlSearch");
                if (catUrlComp) {
                    return catUrlComp.value;
                }
                return "";
            }

            function getKeyWordVal() {
                var keywordComp;

                keywordComp = document.getElementById("keyword");
                if (keywordComp) {
                    return keywordComp.value;
                }
                return "";
            }

            function sendAjaxToAdTech(adURL, resCont) {
                var xhttp = null;
                try {
                    xhttp = new XMLHttpRequest;
                } catch (e) {
                    var msxml = ['MSXML2.XMLHTTP.3.0', 'MSXML2.XMLHTTP',
                        'Microsoft.XMLHTTP'];
                    for (var i = 0, len = msxml.length; i < len; ++i) {
                        try {
                            xhttp = new ActiveXObject(msxml[i]);
                            break;
                        } catch (e) {
                        }
                    }
                }

                xhttp.onreadystatechange = function () {
                    if (xhttp.readyState == 4 && xhttp.status == 200) {
                        resCont.innerHTML = xhttp.responseText;
                        resCont.classList.remove("hidden");
                    }
                };
                try {
                    xhttp.open("GET", adURL + getAdParams(), true);
                    xhttp.setRequestHeader("Content-type", "application/x-www-form-urlencoded");
                    xhttp.send();
                } catch (e) {
                    return;
                }
            }
        }
    })();
</script>
</div>

	getCookie = function(a_name) {
   		if (document.cookie.length > 0) {
   			begin = document.cookie.indexOf(" " + a_name + "=");
   		if (begin != -1) {
   			begin += a_name.length + 2;
   			end = document.cookie.indexOf(";", begin);
   			if (end == -1)
   				end = document.cookie.length;
   			return unescape(document.cookie.substring(begin, end));
   		}else{
   			begin = document.cookie.indexOf(a_name + "=");
   			if(begin != -1){
   				begin += a_name.length + 1;
   				end = document.cookie.indexOf(";", begin);
   				if (end == -1)
   					end = document.cookie.length;
   				return unescape(document.cookie.substring(begin, end));
   			}
   		}
   	}
   	return null;
   };

            	    				for ( var i = 0; i < localValueSplit.length; ++ i ) {

        	    		  		  		var position  =  ( row - 1 ) * 4;
            	    					applyBxSlider(position);
            	    					if (!Snapdeal.WidgetLogger.isIntervalActive()) {
            	                            Snapdeal.WidgetLogger.fireWidgetLog()
            	                        }
        	    		  	  		}
        	    				}else{
	        	    					try{
	        	    						parent	.addClass('hidden');
	        	    					}catch(e){
        	    					}
        	    				}
        	    		 	 }else{

<script type="text/javascript">
(function(){
	getCookie = function(a_name) {
   		if (document.cookie.length > 0) {
   			begin = document.cookie.indexOf(" " + a_name + "=");
   		if (begin != -1) {
   			begin += a_name.length + 2;
   			end = document.cookie.indexOf(";", begin);
   			if (end == -1)
   				end = document.cookie.length;
   			return unescape(document.cookie.substring(begin, end));
   		}else{
   			begin = document.cookie.indexOf(a_name + "=");
   			if(begin != -1){
   				begin += a_name.length + 1;
   				end = document.cookie.indexOf(";", begin);
   				if (end == -1)
   					end = document.cookie.length;
   				return unescape(document.cookie.substring(begin, end));
   			}
   		}
   	}
   	return null;
   };

   	var noOfRows= "3";
  	var rows = noOfRows.split(',');
	var row = 0;

	getAdtechContent();
	
  	function getAdtechContent(){
  		var adSpaceIdArr = [];
  		var adSpaceIdArrUrl = [];

			email = email.substring(1, email.length-1);
		}else{
			email = '';
		}

   			var row = parseInt(rows[i].trim());
			var currPage= parseInt((row*4)/20) + 1;
			++rowIndex;
			var adSpaceId  = 'sd-bn-975X140-'+ currPage +'-'+row;
			var adSpaceIdUrl  = 'sd-bn-975X140-'+"1"+'-'+rowIndex;
			var pageNumber =  Snapdeal.productGrid && Snapdeal.productGrid.getPageNumber();
			if(pageNumber == undefined && currPage == 1){
				adSpaceIdArrUrl.push(adSpaceIdUrl);
				adSpaceIdArr.push(adSpaceId);
			}
			if( parseInt(pageNumber) === parseInt(currPage) ){
				if( parseInt(pageNumber) > parseInt(currPage)  ){
					adSpaceIdArrUrl = [];adSpaceIdArrUrl.length = 0;
					adSpaceIdArr = [];adSpaceIdArr.length = 0;
				}	
				adSpaceIdArrUrl.push(adSpaceIdUrl);
				adSpaceIdArr.push(adSpaceId);
			}
			var position  =  ( row - 1 ) * 4;
  		}	
	   	
	   	function appendBanner(position){
			var response = $(xhttp.responseText);
   			++resIndex;
			if(response[resIndex] === undefined || response[resIndex] === '' || response.filter('.bannerWrapper')[resIndex] == '' || response.filter('.bannerWrapper')[resIndex] == undefined){
			 	document.getElementsByClassName('adtechSearchConatinerBanner').className = "hidden";
			}else if((adSpaceIdArr.length === parseInt(1)  || adSpaceIdArr.length >= parseInt(1) ) && response.filter('.bannerWrapper').length  ===  parseInt(1) ){		
				var parent = getContainer ($, response.filter('.wrapperAdtech')[0]);
				sessionStorage.setItem('creativeDataSearch','');
				sessionStorage.setItem('creativeDataSearch',response.filter('.creativeContainer').text());
				position  -=  1;
				if(!!$("#modelNumberSearch").val()){
					position = parseInt(position) + 1;
				}
				parent	.insertBefore ( $('.product-tuple-listing[data-js-pos="' + (position + 1) + '"]:first-child') );
				parent	.removeClass('hidden');
				Snapdeal.omni.fire("searchAdtechBannerOmni", {});
			}
			else{
				var parent = getContainer ($, response.filter('.wrapperAdtech')[resIndex]);

				parent	.removeClass('hidden');
				Snapdeal.omni.fire("searchAdtechBannerOmni", {});
			}

					xhttp = new ActiveXObject(msxml[i]);
					break;

		}
